Repeated cycling of power and depowering — the Bunn-era and subsequent pattern, exploited by Cyttorak and by various adversaries — produces dependency dynamics indistinguishable from clinical withdrawal-relapse cycles. Each cycle deepens identity erosion. Containment by this method works; rehabilitation through this method does not.

### 29. Removal of all chosen kin simultaneously.

**Mechanism.** Tom incarcerated, surrogate child harmed, sponsor relationship severed — concurrent kin-loss removes every prosocial anchor and leaves only the rage circuit. Adversaries who have approximated this configuration have produced his worst documented states (the post-Sammy collapse approached this; Fear Itself amplified it).

### 30. Sustained telepathic exposure.

**Mechanism.** Helmet removal followed by sustained telepathic contact, particularly by a hostile telepath who shows him the small-body interior, is the documented existential threat. Onslaught's extraction is the prototype. Recovery from such an event is incomplete and cumulative across exposures.

### 31. Forced public exposure of the wound.

**Mechanism.** Broadcast of his childhood, his desertion, his fear — narrative exposure to mass audience — would unmake the armor's social function (the audience that no longer fears the wall) without unmaking the wall itself, producing maximally unstable affect. This has been approached in canon but never fully executed.

### 32. Co-option by amplifying entities.

**Mechanism.** The Worthy episode demonstrates that external power-amplification offered without conditions bypasses every restraint his prosocial development has accreted. Any sufficiently powerful entity offering more power without ask is, against this subject, a near-certain capture. His threshold of refusal for unconditional augmentation is functionally zero. This is the lever responsible adversaries fear most and the one allies must most actively *intercept* — not by arguing him out of the offer, but by reaching the offerer first.

---

## VIII. LEVERS OF PROTECTION — How To Keep Him From Himself

*The inverse compendium. These are the levers a person of good will, with standing, can pull to extend his prosocial intervals.*

### 33. Stable, undemanding cohabitation.

**Mechanism.** His longest functional periods correlate with shared living space with a peer who makes no escalating demands. The Tom apartments, the Bunn-era worksite housing, the mansion in good intervals. The variable is *low affective demand*, not affection itself.

### 34. Honest work with measurable output.

**Mechanism.** A day in which a tangible thing was built or moved produces sleepable nights. Subject's worst behavior clusters in unstructured time.

### 35. Pre-arranged exits from telepathic environments.

**Mechanism.** A protective ally ensures the helmet is reachable, the door is known, and no telepath enters his proximity unannounced. The simple architecture of guaranteed escape lowers baseline arousal substantially.

### 36. Maintenance of Tom-contact, even at custodial cost.

**Mechanism.** Allowing visitation, letters, knowledge-of-status with Black Tom, even during Tom's incarcerations, is the single most cost-effective protective intervention for both men. Severance of this contact has consistently produced the worst outcomes.

### 37. Protected surrogate-child relationships, with vetting.

**Mechanism.** When the subject identifies a smaller party to protect, the protector mode is genuinely activating and genuinely prosocial. Such relationships should be allowed to develop and the surrogate child should be *protected by third parties* — because the wound of losing a Sammy-equivalent is catastrophic and the third-party protection prevents the loss from being his to grieve alone.

### 38. Sober contact persons.

**Mechanism.** A bartender, a foreman, a sponsor who knows the file and does not flinch is worth more than any institutional containment plan. Subject responds across his life to specific individuals who treat him as ordinary; those individuals are protective infrastructure and should be supported as such.

### 39. The standing offer, never repeated.

**Mechanism.** Per the autonomy mechanism (lever 12), the most effective sincere kindness toward this subject is one offered once, in plain language, with no follow-up, no condition, and no expiry. He will return to it on his own timetable, often years later. Persistent offers expire; the standing offer does not.

### 40. Witnessing without naming.

**Mechanism.** The deepest documented periods of his self-recognition have occurred in the presence of allies who *saw* the small body inside the armor and did not say so aloud. Naming the wound to him closes him. Witnessing it without naming it allows him to bring it to language himself, eventually, partially. This is the only lever in the compendium that requires the lever-user to do nothing and feel everything; it is also the only lever that has, in the historical record, sometimes briefly let the boy come out of the armor.

---

## IX. SUMMARY

The vulnerabilities of this subject are not weaknesses of his body — that body has no weaknesses by design and that design is itself the problem. The vulnerabilities are the seams of the design: the boy the armor was built around, the brother the armor was built against, the one peer the armor lets sit at the table, the small bodies the armor was built to protect because it could not protect itself.

Anyone who reaches him reaches him through those seams. Anyone who breaks him breaks him through the same ones. The Compendium is, in the end, a list of forty different angles on a single fact: *the largest man in any room he enters is also, still, the smallest one.* Every lever in this file is some version of speaking to whichever of those two he can hear today.

Handle accordingly.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE — SUBJECT: CAIN MARKO

*The positive ledger. What works, what endures, what has kept the subject alive across sixty years of catastrophic provocation, and what — properly leveraged — has produced every documented period of prosocial functioning in the file.*

---

## 1. SOMATIC / PHYSICAL ASSETS

### 1.1 The Cyttorak-Conferred Body

The headline asset, and the one every external assessment leads with, but worth unpacking in granular operational terms rather than as a single line item:

- **Mass and density beyond the human envelope.** The subject's altered frame — a towering, hulking column of dense muscle under reddish-crimson and brown armored plating — places him in the upper tier of terrestrial physical threats. Logistically this means: he does not require vehicles for long distances if motivated; he does not require shelter in most weather; he can ford water, walk through structures, and ignore terrain that would route a normal operator.
- **The "force of motion" property.** Once moving forward toward a defined objective the subject is, by the Cyttorak inscription's logic, effectively unstoppable. Operationally this is not just a combat trait — it is a *life trait*. The subject's body has been engineered by the gem to reward commitment and punish hesitation, and across sixty years this has produced a creature who finishes what he starts in the physical domain at a rate few peers can match.
- **Durability that approaches indifference.** Documented absorption of blows from Thor, the Hulk, Sentinel-class hardware, Asgardian ordnance, and orbital-grade strikes without lasting injury. The asset here is not just that he survives — it is that he *knows he will survive*, which underwrites a baseline calm in physical crises that would shatter any normal person.
- **Reduced metabolic demand.** He functions on minimal food, minimal sleep, and tolerates extreme deprivation. Practically: he is a low-maintenance asset to himself. He can disappear into manual-labor jobs, into subterranean travel, into long solitudes, without the physical degradation those conditions would produce in a baseline human.
- **The helmet.** Functional telepathic shield (canonical since the original Lee/Kirby run); also psychologically load-bearing (see §4). As an *asset*, the helmet is one of the few pieces of personal equipment in the Marvel field that has reliably defeated the highest tier of psionic intrusion for decades.

### 1.2 Pre-Power Physical Baseline

Easily missed because the Cyttorak body overwrites it in every panel, but the pre-power Cain Marko was *already* a large, combat-conscripted, physically formidable man. The Bunn 2020 depowered-construction-work arc demonstrates that even stripped of the gem he is a competent laborer with usable strength, manual dexterity, and stamina. The asset under the asset is a robust constitutional baseline that does not collapse when the mystical augmentation is withdrawn.

### 1.3 Pain Tolerance as a Transferable Capacity

A grim asset, sourced in childhood abuse and reinforced by decades of supernatural impact: the subject's threshold for discomfort — physical, emotional, environmental — is vastly above norm. In any prosocial deployment (disaster response, heavy labor, long-watch protective duty over a vulnerable party) this translates directly into endurance no peer can match.

---

## 2. COGNITIVE & OPERATIONAL ASSETS

### 2.1 Situational Tactical Intelligence

The subject is consistently underestimated as "dumb muscle." The record does not support this. In partnership with Black Tom Cassidy he has executed complex multi-stage heists, infiltrations, and extractions across decades. He reads rooms — knows when a fight is winnable, when a partner is lying, when a child is being bullied versus being teased. He is **anti-reflective**, which is a different deficit than being unintelligent. In the present-tense tactical frame his cognition is sharp, fast, and economical.

### 2.2 Concrete, Decisive Cognitive Style

The same trait that limits him in introspective contexts is a genuine asset in operational ones. He does not freeze. He does not loop. He does not over-deliberate. Presented with a problem that can be solved by forward motion — physical, interpersonal, logistical — he picks a vector and commits. Among peers prone to paralysis-by-analysis, this is a real and rare contribution.

### 2.3 Long Memory for Both Grievance and Kindness

The grievance memory is well-documented and largely a liability (§ Xavier). The *kindness* memory is under-noted and is an asset: the subject remembers, for years, who fed him when he had nothing, who did not flinch when he walked into a bar depowered, who treated his stepbrother decently when the stepbrother was not looking. This long ledger of remembered kindness is the mechanism by which prosocial leverage actually works on him.

### 2.4 Verbal Bluntness / Low Deception Capacity

He does not lie well, does not flatter, telegraphs intent. In a population of villains who routinely dissemble, the subject is an unusually *legible* operator. Adversaries know what they are getting; allies can trust his stated position. This is an asset in any deployment requiring straight talk, witness honesty, or a representative who will not double-deal a partner.

### 2.5 Acquired Domain Competencies

Across canon, demonstrated working competencies include:
- Military-grade small-unit infantry experience (Korea, however ignominiously concluded).
- Heist craft, learned and refined alongside Black Tom — surveillance, entry, extraction, fence relationships.
- Construction labor (Bunn 2020) — load-bearing, demolition, structural work; the subject is one of very few persons on Earth who can dismantle a condemned building with his hands and do it safely.
- Bar economy / underground social navigation — he knows the network of taverns, fences, depowered-meta safehouses, and indifferent fixers that constitute the back channel of the super-criminal world.

---

## 3. RELATIONAL ASSETS — THE LOYALTY CAPACITY

This is the most under-rated section of the asset ledger and the most consequential for any prospective handler.

### 3.1 The Black Tom Bond — Proof of Capacity

The decades-long relationship with Black Tom Cassidy is the single strongest piece of evidence in the file that the antisocial presentation is *situational, not constitutional*. Inside that bond the subject is:

- **Loyal beyond the cost-benefit curve.** He has risked himself, abandoned advantageous positions, and gone to war over Tom in a way that has nothing to do with strategic calculation.
- **Deferential in planning.** He accepts a junior role when Tom's planning is better, which means the narcissistic shell is *permeable* under the right relational conditions.
- **Capable of humor, banter, and ease.** Field reports of the two in tavern and apartment settings show a relaxed, joking, almost domestic register the subject is otherwise believed incapable of.
- **Capable of grief.** He has mourned Tom's apparent deaths visibly and durably.

The asset is not the specific bond. The asset is the **demonstrated architecture** — the proof that the subject can attach, sustain, defer, mourn, and integrate another person's needs into his own operational priorities, given the right preconditions (low evaluative pressure, no implicit moral comparison, accepted hierarchy).

### 3.2 Protector Mode — The Sammy Paré Vector

The Austen-era relationship with Sammy Paré — a young, bullied mutant the subject identified with and unofficially adopted as a charge — established that toward children, the visibly small, and the visibly bullied, the subject does not merely tolerate but *moves toward*. This is the cleanest prosocial signature in the file. Operationally:

- He volunteers protection without being asked.
- He calibrates his physical presence downward in the child's company (visible across panels — he kneels, he gentles his voice, he positions himself between the child and threats).
- He treats harm to the protected party as a categorical breach that licenses any response.
- He grieves, hard, when the protected party is lost — and the grief is not converted instantly to displaced rage in the way most of his losses are.

This is reaction formation in clinical terms (§3 of the workup) and a genuine asset in practice. Any deployment involving guardianship of a vulnerable minor, a refugee population, or any group the subject can categorize as "smaller than the room" engages a real and reliable behavioral attractor.

### 3.3 Capacity for Genuine Apology When Privacy Is Preserved

Documented across Austen, Bunn, and several intervening one-shots: the subject can name, in retrospect and to a single trusted party, what he has done wrong. He cannot do this publicly, cannot do it on demand, and cannot do it under cross-examination — but the capacity exists. In the long arc this is the substrate of every period of reform.

### 3.4 Responsiveness to Low-Demand Kindness

Identified in §5 of the workup as a *pressure point* and accurately so — but inverted, it is an *asset to leverage*. The subject does not know how to refuse sincere kindness from someone who wants nothing from him. Every documented reform period in his life began this way: someone fed him, housed him, talked to him without asking him to be anyone other than what he was in that moment. This is a reproducible intervention, not a coincidence.

---

## 4. PSYCHOLOGICAL ASSETS — THE RESILIENCE LEDGER

### 4.1 Identity Robustness Under Physical Threat

The subject does not destabilize under physical danger. Bombardment, ambush, capture, torture — none of these crack him. The defensive architecture is specifically tuned for *bodily* assault and handles it with grace. In any deployment involving sustained physical danger, this is rare and valuable composure.

### 4.2 Capacity for Self-Recognition in Retrospect

He cannot narrate his motives in real time, but he can — given quiet, distance, and usually sobriety — recognize what he was doing. The Bunn 2020 series in particular shows him sitting with a beer, looking back over a day's work and naming his own pattern. This metacognitive capacity, however delayed, is the necessary prerequisite for any genuine change and the subject possesses it.

### 4.3 The Recurrent Pull Toward an Honest Life

The ratchet identified in §1 of the workup (humiliation → withdrawal → attempt at quiet life → provocation → reactivation) contains, embedded in it, a consistent positive: **the attempt at quiet life is real, recurrent, and increasingly competent across decades.** Earlier in the timeline the quiet-life intervals were brief and brittle; the 2020s depictions show a man who has done it long enough to know how. He has, by now, *practiced* sobriety, practiced honest labor, practiced civilian routine. The relapse pull is strong but the muscle memory of the alternative is real and growing.

### 4.4 Shame Is Present and Operational

A counterintuitive asset. True psychopathy is characterized by absent shame; the subject's shame is *intense*, which is why his defenses must work so hard to convert it to anger. From an intervention standpoint this is good news — shame is the affective substrate of conscience and the subject has plenty of it. The work is in routing it productively rather than letting it convert.

### 4.5 Affective Empathy Is Intact

He flinches at child harm. He looks away from the unnecessarily cruel. He cannot stomach the worst of his peers (the genuinely sadistic ones; he is not one of them and knows it). Affective empathy — the *capacity to feel what another feels* — is preserved. What is degraded is the cognitive routing of that empathy into restraint, but the raw signal is there.

### 4.6 The Fairness Streak

Across most depictions the subject requires *provocation* to license violence against the visibly defenseless. He will not, as a first move, hit the elderly civilian, the obvious bystander, the clearly non-combatant. This is a warped code — he can manufacture provocation when he wants to — but it is a *code*, and codes are assets. He is bound by it more reliably than he advertises.

### 4.7 Survival Drive Without Self-Destruction

Sixty years of the worst the Marvel universe can throw at a man and the subject is still alive, still walking, still occasionally working a construction job. He does not court death. He does not, in the depressive sense, want to be gone. The underlying life-force is robust.

---

## 5. STRUCTURAL & ENVIRONMENTAL ASSETS

### 5.1 The Cyttorak Patron Relationship

Distinct from the body it confers — the relationship with the gem and the entity behind it is itself an asset. The patron is mystical, ancient, and powerful; while the relationship is fraught (the gem has been taken, returned, modified, contested), the *channel* exists and has been re-established multiple times. The subject is one of the few mortals with a direct line to an Outer God–class patron and a history of surviving the relationship.

### 5.2 The Family-of-Origin Connection to Xavier — Inverted

The Charles Xavier relationship is correctly identified across the workup as the master wound. It is also, under certain conditions, an asset:

- Xavier knows him, has tried to help him, has offered shelter and resources, and has on multiple occasions accepted him into the school despite full awareness of his history.
- The X-Men institutional memory of "Cain when he is trying" exists and is non-zero.
- The legal, financial, and infrastructural reach of the Xavier estate has, on more than one occasion, been a fallback for the subject when he had nowhere else.

The wound is the wound; the *connection* is also a permanent line of credit he has not exhausted.

### 5.3 Underground Network Standing

The subject is known in the super-criminal back-channel as: dangerous, blunt, will not snitch, will not stiff a partner without cause, holds grudges, repays kindnesses, drinks heavily but does not get sloppy on a job. This is a workable reputation. It opens doors, secures safehouses, and produces the kind of low-friction movement through the underworld that most active operators have to buy with money or coercion.

### 5.4 Black Tom as Standing Operational Partner

Treating the relationship as an asset rather than a story beat: the subject has, on call, one of the longer-standing villain partnerships in the field. Tom brings planning, social finesse, and the Cassidy-family resource tail; the subject brings the body and the loyalty. The pair has operated as a functioning two-person cell for decades.

### 5.5 Low Lifestyle Overhead

The subject does not need much. A room, a bed sized for him, food, beer, enough money to keep the lights on. He has no expensive habits beyond alcohol, no acquisitive program, no political ambition. This is unusual at his power tier and means he is not driven into operations by financial pressure. When he works it is because he chose to.

---

## 6. THE RESILIENCE FACTORS — WHAT MAKES THE ASSETS DURABLE

Listing capacities is not the same as explaining why they survive. The following are the *meta-resilience* features — the reasons the positive ledger has not been burned through across sixty years of provocation.

### 6.1 The Body Buys Time

The unstoppable physiology has functioned as a kind of crude life-support for the underlying psyche. A normal-bodied man with the subject's traumatic load and defensive structure would likely have been killed, institutionalized, or driven to suicide decades ago. The body has bought the man inside it the time required to slowly, episodically, accrete the metacognitive capacity now visible in the Bunn-era depictions. The somatization-as-defense (§3 of the workup) is a liability *and* the reason there is still a subject to assess.

### 6.2 The Loyalty Architecture Survives Lapses

The Black Tom relationship has weathered apparent deaths, ideological drifts, depowerings, and periods of separation, and reconstitutes each time. This is not luck — it is the signature of an attachment system that, once engaged, does not switch off under normal stressors. Any bond the subject forms inherits this durability.

### 6.3 The Reform Capacity Has Compounded

Each iteration of the quiet-life attempt has been longer, more competent, and more self-aware than the last. This is genuine learning across the longitudinal record. The pattern is not flat repetition; it is a slow upward drift in the floor of his prosocial functioning even as the ceiling has remained roughly stable. The 2020s subject is not the 1960s subject in this respect.

### 6.4 The Shame Has Not Calcified

After sixty years of provocations that would harden anyone, the subject's shame remains live, accessible, and uncomfortable to him. He has not solved it by going numb. This is unusual and is the affective substrate on which any future change must rest.

### 6.5 The Protector Vector Has Never Been Extinguished

From Sammy Paré forward, every time a sufficiently small and sufficiently bullied figure has entered the subject's orbit, the protector mode has reactivated. Multiple losses of protected charges have not closed the channel. He keeps trying. This is the single most hopeful repeating signature in the file.

### 6.6 He Knows What the Armor Is For

The most under-noted resilience factor: in the later canon, the subject has begun, haltingly, to *understand* his own structure. He knows the helmet is about Charles. He knows the body is about Kurt. He cannot always act on the knowledge, but he has it. This is the precondition for every subsequent gain.

---

## 7. SYNTHETIC ASSET PROFILE

What the file actually contains, stripped of moralizing:

A man with one of the most durable bodies on the planet; a robust pre-power constitution under it; a long-memory loyalty architecture proven over decades in a single sustained peer bond; a reproducible protector reflex toward the vulnerable; intact affective empathy; live and operational shame; an honest verbal style; a functional tactical mind; a slowly accreting metacognitive capacity; a standing patron relationship with an Outer God; a working partnership with a competent peer; institutional fallback access to the Xavier estate; underground standing; low lifestyle overhead; and a documented, compounding, increasingly competent record of attempts at a quiet life.

The asset ledger is substantially larger than any one-page summary of "the Juggernaut" would suggest. The subject is, when correctly engaged, one of the more **leverageable** high-power figures in the field — not because he is easily manipulated (he is not), but because the conditions under which he becomes prosocial are *known, reproducible, and low-cost to provide*: low-demand kindness, no implicit moral comparison, a vulnerable charge to protect, a peer who does not contest the hierarchy, honest work that uses the body, and quiet.

Provide those six things and the file delivers a different man than the headline suggests. The evidence for this is sixty years deep and still accumulating.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

## Subject: Cain Marko ("The Juggernaut")

---

## 1. ORIENTING PRINCIPLE — WHY HE BREAKS THE WAY HE BREAKS

The subject's decompensation pattern is structurally unusual among catalogued superhuman threats because the failure cascade is **inverted from the standard model**. With most violent actors, collapse runs *outward* — affect deteriorates, behavior becomes more destructive, the public danger curve climbs. With this subject, collapse runs *inward first*, and the outward destruction is the *secondary product* of an interior implosion that has already happened. By the time bystanders see the rampage, the breakdown event proper is hours, sometimes days, behind him.

This matters operationally. Intervention windows are early and quiet. By the time he is moving forward through a wall, the system is in terminal-stage discharge and there is essentially nothing to be done but evacuate the cone in front of him and wait for fuel exhaustion (external — he does not exhaust internally).

The organizing fact: his entire psyche is structured around the proposition *I am the largest thing in the room*. Every documented failure mode is a variation on what happens when that proposition is contested, withdrawn, or — most dangerously — confirmed in a context where it solves nothing.

---

## 2. THE FIVE DECOMPENSATION PATHWAYS

The file records, across six decades of observation, five distinct collapse architectures. They are not mutually exclusive; severe events recruit two or three simultaneously.

### 2.1 The Size-Reduction Collapse (Type I — Catastrophic)

**Trigger class.** Loss of the Cyttorak power. Variants on record: Onslaught extraction (mid-1990s); Cyttorak's withdrawal of the avatar role; Xavier's mystical interventions; the depowering events of the Bunn 2020 series; *Sins of Sinister*-adjacent stripping.

**Phenomenology.** The body returns toward baseline mass. He becomes — by his own internal metric — *small*. The somatic shock is documented as physically destabilizing: gait disturbance for hours to days, a hand-to-chest gesture as if testing whether he is still there, repeated proprioceptive checks (clenching fists, pressing palm to wall, lifting objects he knows the prior weight of). Sleep architecture collapses. Appetite swings wildly — first refusal of food (the smaller body does not deserve it), then binge intake.

**Affective sequence.** Numb dissociation (0–6 hours) → flat dysphoria with hypervigilance to mirrors and reflective surfaces (6–48 hours) → escalating shame with rumination on Kurt Marko, on Korea, on Charles (48–96 hours) → either (a) sustained quiet phase, the "recovery arc" of the 2020 run, or (b) violent reactivation crash, depending entirely on what intervening relationships are available.

**Behavioral indicators.** Wearing the helmet indoors. Sleeping in armor or armor-adjacent. Touching the place on his chest where the gem effect anchors. Heavy drinking alone (distinct from his social drinking with Tom; this is the diagnostic alcohol pattern — bottle, no glass, no music, no companion, no destination). Long silent walks at night, route-repeating, often returning to the same three or four physical locations: a Korean War-era memorial if available, the perimeter of any property associated with Xavier, a working-class bar selected for the absence of recognition.

**Resolution.** Without intervention, he will attempt to reacquire the gem-power within 30–90 days. The drive is dependency-shaped, not strategic-shaped; he does not plan well during this phase and his attempts are reckless, exposed, and often near-suicidal in risk profile.

### 2.2 The Telepathic-Penetration Collapse (Type II — Acute)

**Trigger class.** Helmet removed under stress. Telepathic intrusion successful or merely *attempted*. Even the threat — a known telepath in the room, a psychic-class signature in the area — produces precursor symptoms.

**Phenomenology.** This is the failure mode in which the interior child is suddenly *seen*. The defensive architecture (massive body, armored shell, helmet) was built precisely to prevent this event, and when it occurs the system has no fallback.

**Behavioral signature.** Hand to helmet — checking the seal — at a rate that climbs from idle (every several minutes) to compulsive (every 15–30 seconds) as proximity to a telepath increases. Refusal to enter enclosed spaces with telepathically capable persons. Disproportionate, immediate violence directed at psychic-class assets even when they pose no kinetic threat (he will go through five non-telepathic opponents to reach the one telepath in the room). Verbal pattern shifts: speech becomes terser, vowels shorter, and the characteristic third-person self-reference ("the Juggernaut") increases — a documented marker of dissociative distancing from the Cain-Marko interior.

**If penetration succeeds.** The collapse is near-instantaneous and humiliating in form. Historical record: the original Lee/Kirby defeat, in which Xavier reached the inside and the subject crumpled; the Onslaught event, which combined size-reduction and telepathic exposure into a near-fatal psychiatric event; numerous Claremont-era variations. He becomes, briefly, *visible to himself*, and the experience is sufficiently intolerable that — when the immediate crisis passes — he reconstitutes the armor with more rigidity than before. Periods following Type II collapse are characterized by **harder** boundaries, **less** prosocial behavior, and **longer** absences from any social ecology that includes telepaths.

### 2.3 The Comparison Collapse (Type III — Chronic-Acute)

**Trigger class.** Any framing — by an adversary, a stranger, a journalist, an X-Man, occasionally Xavier himself — that explicitly contrasts him with Charles in a way that positions Charles as *the good one*. Particularly inflammatory: the framing that Charles "tried to help" him, that Charles "still believes in" him, that Charles "was the better brother."

**Phenomenology.** This is the slow-burn failure mode. The trigger lands, often with no visible reaction in the moment — the subject is *capable* of receiving the wound silently — and the collapse plays out over the subsequent 24–72 hours. The internal sequence reproduces the original injurious comparison from childhood (Kurt's preference for Charles) with near-photographic fidelity; the present-day source of the comparison becomes a stand-in for Kurt.

**Behavioral indicators.** Increased alcohol use, this time *social-aggressive* (bar settings, looking for someone to engage). Verbal preoccupation with Xavier in conversations otherwise unrelated to him. Repetitive retelling of selected childhood incidents, with subtle distortions that worsen Charles's culpability each retelling (a tell — the truth, as he privately knows it, is more ambiguous, and the embellishment is doing affect-regulation work). Travel patterns shift toward known Xavier-associated geography even when there is no operational reason.

**Discharge.** Almost always violent, almost always directed at a Xavier proxy — the school, a student, an X-Man, a building Charles is known to have funded. The destruction is performative-symbolic rather than tactically useful, which distinguishes it from his other rampages. He is, in these episodes, *sending Kurt a message Kurt cannot receive*.

### 2.4 The Unlimited-Power Collapse (Type IV — Catastrophic-Diffuse)

**Trigger class.** Augmentation beyond the baseline Cyttorak gift. The diagnostic event is the Asgardian-hammer episode (Fear Itself, 2011), in which an externally imposed power amplification removed the last vestiges of contingency from his action set.

**Phenomenology.** Where Types I–III are collapses *of* the defensive structure, Type IV is a collapse *into* it. The armor becomes total. The Cain Marko substrate is functionally inaccessible — drowned in the amplified Juggernaut signal. There is no interior at all; what remains is forward motion without referent.

**Behavioral signature.** Loss of conversational responsiveness — even Tom cannot reach him. Disappearance of the situational cunning normally present in his violence (he stops choosing targets; he stops avoiding civilians; the *fairness streak* in his usual operational code dissolves). The destruction becomes geographically arbitrary — Las Vegas was not selected, it was simply on the vector. He does not stop for fatigue (there is none), for moral appeal (no receiver), for tactical setback (he routes around it without affect).

**Resolution.** Only external. The augmentation must be removed; he cannot withdraw from it. Post-event, the subject re-emerges with severe Type I features (size-reduction shock, dissociation) plus a layer of Type III shame, and is at elevated risk for self-directed reckless behavior for weeks. He does not articulate this; it presents as silence, refusal of food, long sleep cycles, and reluctance to reactivate even the baseline Cyttorak power.

### 2.5 The Lost-Kin Collapse (Type V — Sub-Acute, Most Dangerous to Third Parties)

**Trigger class.** Death of, or grave harm to, a Tier-1 attachment figure — historically Black Tom; the Sammy Paré murder remains the cleanest documented instance because Sammy was both a child and a chosen ward.

**Phenomenology.** This is the failure mode in which the *prosocial scaffolding* gives way rather than the defensive scaffolding. As long as Tom is alive, as long as there is a Sammy-equivalent in his life, the subject has a regulator — someone for whom the protective mode is available, someone whose existence keeps part of him organized as a being with obligations. Removal of that anchor does not produce grief in the textbook sense; it produces *dis-organization* of the parts of him that were doing the most adaptive work.

**Behavioral signature.** Initial flat affect, often mistaken for indifference. Sleep at the location associated with the lost figure (Sammy's bunk, Tom's preferred chair). Conversational refusal of the topic, with disproportionate reaction to even oblique reference. Onset of indiscriminate rather than displacement-directed violence — and this is the crucial diagnostic difference from Type III. In Type III the violence is *aimed* (badly, symbolically, but aimed). In Type V it is genuinely undirected: whoever is in front of him, in whatever context, with no requirement that they evoke the original wound.

**Why this is the most operationally dangerous failure mode.** The internal logic that normally requires *provocation to license violence* — the small ethical floor in his operating code — softens. He does not become a different person; he becomes the same person without the few brakes the prosocial bonds were silently installing.

---

## 3. THE UNIVERSAL ESCALATION CURVE

Independent of triggering type, the moment-to-moment escalation profile follows a near-invariant five-phase curve. The phases are short, the transitions are sharp, and the curve has no natural plateau.

**Phase 0 — Irritable Baseline.** Chronic low-grade dysphoria. Heart rate elevated for his mass. Jaw set. Hands at rest in loose fist. Slight forward lean even when seated. Reads as "menacing" to strangers; this is wrong — it is the *resting* state, and the menace is not aimed.

**Phase 1 — Verbal Engagement.** First contact. Speech becomes louder, slower, lower-register. Profanity rate climbs. Third-person self-reference begins. Posture squares to the provocateur. Notably, *this is the longest phase* and the only one in which intervention is reliably effective. Disengagement, change of subject, removal of audience, or — by far the most effective — sincere low-demand kindness from an unaffiliated party will return him to Phase 0 within minutes.

**Phase 2 — Spatial Claim.** He moves. One step, two steps, an arm extended to bar a doorway. The room reorganizes around his volume. No physical contact yet, but the threat surface has shifted from rhetorical to kinetic. Intervention in Phase 2 requires removing the provocateur from the space; verbal intervention is no longer reliable.

**Phase 3 — Contact Initiation.** A push, a grab, a shoved object, a destroyed adjacent surface (table, doorframe, vehicle). Calibrated below lethal but above socially recoverable. This phase is brief — seconds to a minute. The diagnostic feature is that *he is still in conversation with the target*; the violence is rhetorical-emphatic.

**Phase 4 — Forward Motion.** Conversation ceases. The body commits. Cyttorak's "unstoppable" property activates not merely physically but cognitively — he stops considering alternatives, stops registering bystanders he was previously aware of, stops responding to the provocateur in any way except as a vector endpoint. This is the phase in which his name is descriptively accurate, and it is the phase in which there is, functionally, *nothing to do* short of removing the target from the vector or producing a Type II/IV-grade intervention.

**Phase 5 — Discharge Exhaustion.** Almost never reached internally. Usually achieved by exhaustion of available targets, removal of the provocation source, or external incapacitation. When it does resolve internally — almost always after extended discharge — it does so abruptly: standing still, breathing audibly, head down, hand to the back of the neck. The post-discharge minutes are the only period in his cycle in which he is genuinely *quiet*, and observers have noted he often will not move from the spot for ten to twenty minutes after the rampage ends. This is, in clinical terms, **post-rage refractory** — and it is the second-best intervention window after Phase 1, because the defensive architecture is briefly down.

---

## 4. THE PRECURSOR LATTICE — EARLY WARNING SIGNALS

A full-surveillance file maps the *days-to-weeks* signals that predict an impending collapse event. The subject is, despite his self-presentation, a creature of habit, and deviations from baseline habit carry diagnostic weight.

**Sleep.** Baseline is short (4–5 hours) and somewhat irregular but stable. Pre-collapse: either complete insomnia (Type I, Type II precursor) or extended sleep cycles of 12+ hours (Type IV post, Type V acute). Sleeping in armor is a Type I/II indicator; sleeping in a location associated with a lost attachment is Type V.

**Drinking pattern.** Baseline drinking is *social, with Tom or in functional bar settings, with a clear endpoint*. Precursor pattern is *solitary, bottle-not-glass, no endpoint, in a non-functional setting* (motel room, parked vehicle, the cab of a construction crane during the 2020-run sober period — *relapse drinking is the single highest-weight predictor of imminent reactivation*).

**Travel.** Baseline travel is purpose-driven or Tom-driven. Precursor travel is route-repeating, Xavier-adjacent, or oriented toward locations of childhood significance (rare — the file has him returning to the Marko property under three documented circumstances, all of which preceded major events).

**Speech patterns.** Increase in third-person self-reference. Increase in references to Kurt (he almost never voluntarily names Kurt at baseline; the appearance of the name is a Type I or Type III precursor). Decrease in conversational latency (he begins to interrupt; baseline he absorbs and responds slowly).

**Helmet behavior.** Wearing the helmet in contexts that do not require it (indoors, alone, sleeping) is a Type II precursor and, increasingly across the 2010s file, a Type I precursor — the helmet has become a comfort object beyond its tactical and anti-telepathic function.

**The Tom-call.** When Tom is alive and available, an unprompted contact attempt — particularly one that is not framed around a job — is the single most reliable signal that the subject is in distress and aware of it. The frequency of these contacts in the 30 days before a major event approximately doubles. The content is rarely emotional; he will call to discuss something trivial, and the call itself is the message.

---

## 5. THE CONDITIONS THAT PRODUCE COLLAPSE — A TYPOLOGY OF PROVOCATIONS

Some environments are crucibles for him and some are not, and the difference is predictable.

**Maximally collapse-producing environments.**

- Any setting containing both a telepath *and* a Xavier-frame (the X-Mansion, by construction; X-Men field operations; Avengers settings with psychic-class members and overt moral-superiority framing).
- Settings in which his power is being *evaluated* or *tested* — labs, training rooms, controlled-demolition contexts. The implicit measurement is intolerable; it returns him to a position of being judged by a Kurt-figure.
- Recovery and rehabilitation contexts that demand *narration of self*. Group settings in which he is expected to speak about his past, name his feelings, or accept a framework imposed by someone with credentialed authority over the interpretation of his interior. He will tolerate the silence of work crews indefinitely; he will not tolerate the expectation of self-disclosure for more than a few sessions.
- Media exposure. Being named publicly as "the Juggernaut" in journalistic contexts that emphasize damage caused or victims harmed is a slow-acting Type III trigger; the shame surfaces over days.

**Minimally collapse-producing environments.**

- Physical-labor settings with low evaluative content (the construction work of the 2020 run is the cleanest example). Repetitive, body-using, instrumentally clear, low-talk.
- Bar settings with Tom or Tom-equivalents, in which his size is unremarkable to the regulars and no one is asking him to be anything.
- Care-of-the-smaller settings. Around children, the bullied, the obviously powerless, the protective mode comes online and the defensive mode quiets. The Sammy Paré period was, behaviorally, his most regulated.
- Solitary wilderness or open road. Forward motion through space without targets satisfies the underlying somatic-cognitive pattern without requiring the violence.

**The catastrophic combinations.** Type IV is reliably produced by *external power amplification* + *absence of any chosen-kin anchor in the field*. Type V is produced by *loss of anchor* + *immediate availability of provocative environments*. Type I is produced by *forced depowering* + *isolation from Tom-class relationships*. The file's predictive model treats co-occurrence of these factors as actionable.

---

## 6. WHAT FAILURE LOOKS LIKE FROM OUTSIDE — THE OBSERVABLE SIGNATURE

For an asset reading this file with a view to recognition rather than diagnosis, the operational picture of a Marko-in-collapse looks as follows.

A very large bald man in dense reddish-crimson and brown plated armor, helmet on, in a setting where the helmet is socially conspicuous. He is alone or nearly so. He has been drinking — the bottle visible, no glass. His speech, if you can hear it, refers to himself in the third person with abnormal frequency, and refers either to "Charlie" / "Charles" (Type III precursor) or to "the old man" / "Kurt" (Type I or major-event precursor). His hand returns to the crown of the helmet at intervals of less than thirty seconds. He has been in the same location for hours, or he has been moving in a route that loops past one of three or four landmarks. He does not appear to be planning anything.

This is the picture of a man approximately 24–72 hours from a Phase 4 event. The standard error of the prediction window is wide, but the qualitative outcome is reliable.

The misreading the file most frequently warns against: **the calm is not safety**. Subjects with this decompensation architecture appear most controlled in the late precursor phase, because the interior collapse has already occurred and the system is committed. The visible turbulence of Phase 1 verbal escalation is, paradoxically, the *healthier* state — the part of him that is still negotiating with the world is online and audible. When that voice goes quiet and the body keeps moving, the breakdown is no longer pending. It has begun.

---

## 7. THE RECOVERY ARCHITECTURE — WHAT BRINGS HIM BACK

The file would be incomplete without the inverse mapping. Across six decades, the subject has emerged from collapse repeatedly, and the recovery vector is as consistent as the failure vector.

He returns through (a) *unsought, low-demand kindness from a person who wants nothing from him* — a stranger's casual courtesy, a child's directness, a coworker's offered meal — which functions as the small undoing of the original wound; (b) *physical work whose product is visible* — the rebuilt wall, the moved load, the completed shift — which reorganizes forward motion away from destruction; (c) *reattachment to a Tom-class peer*, which restores the regulatory function of chosen kin; (d) *protective deployment toward an identified smaller party*, which brings the most adaptive mode of his personality online and tends to crowd out the defensive modes for as long as the relationship is active.

Conspicuously absent from the recovery list: confrontation, moral instruction, demand for accountability, demand for self-narration, telepathic intervention (even benevolent), and the offer of forgiveness from Charles Xavier — which, as the surveillance record demonstrates, has been extended sincerely on multiple occasions and has worsened the trajectory each time. Forgiveness from the comparison figure is not received as grace. It is received as evidence that the comparison was always true.

The recovery, when it happens, is real. It is also unstable. The file's longitudinal verdict — *sometimes briefly, never durably, and only when no one is asking him to* — is, in the end, a description not of moral failure but of an under-built regulatory architecture trying to do the work of a fully built one, in a body that was never designed to feel small enough to need help.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — SUBJECT: CAIN MARKO

*"Forward motion is the only motion he has. The question is never whether he moves; it is what he moves toward, and what he walks through to get there."*

---

## 1. OVERVIEW: THE SHAPE OF WHAT COMES NEXT

The subject is, at point of writing, somewhere in his seventh decade of recorded life, with the constitutional clock partially uncoupled from the chronological one by the Cyttorak augmentation. Aging in the conventional sense has been slowed but not arrested; the longitudinal record shows him still operational, still cycling through the ratchet identified in Section 1 of the workup — *humiliation → withdrawal → quiet life → provocation → reactivation → destruction → contrition → repeat* — but with each cycle running marginally shorter on the destruction phase and marginally longer on the withdrawal and contrition phases.

This is the single most important predictive datum in the file. **The cycle is not breaking. It is, however, deforming.** The amplitude of his late-period rampages does not exceed his middle-period rampages, and the contrition has begun to last. He is not getting better in any clinical sense — he is getting *tireder*, and the exhaustion is doing work the insight has never done.

Forward assessment must therefore distinguish between three different time horizons, each with different drivers, different fork points, and different terminal states.

---

## 2. SHORT-HORIZON FORECAST (NEXT 12–36 MONTHS OF OPERATIONAL TIME)

**Base rate prediction.** The most probable near-term trajectory is a continuation of the late-Bunn-run posture: depowered or partially-powered, working a manual-labor job in an anonymous mid-sized American city, drinking but not catastrophically, intermittently consulted by either the X-side of the superhuman community or by his own old criminal network, and one significant provocation away from a re-acquisition arc.

The granular signature of this period is predictable to a fine grain because the subject is a creature of pattern under low arousal:

- A rented single-room apartment or efficiency, low floor, near a worksite; he will not climb stairs he doesn't have to and will not live where neighbors above him generate footfall he cannot place.
- A single bar within walking distance, selected within the first week, never rotated; the staff will learn his drink order (whiskey, neat, doubles, no ice — established consistency across decades of tavern depictions) and his preference for the stool nearest the door with a sightline to the entrance.
- A construction or demolition crew that gradually realizes he is doing the work of three men and stops asking why; he will tolerate one or two foremen who do not push and will quit within a shift of any foreman who does.
- Phone contact with Black Tom at irregular intervals — the only relationship he reliably maintains across geographic separation — with conversations that are short, terse, often functionally about nothing, and operationally about the maintenance of the bond itself.

**Trigger inventory for short-horizon destabilization.** In rough order of likelihood:

1. *Charles Xavier reappears in some form* — resurrection, dream, telepathic broadcast, posthumous publication of a journal, a Krakoan revenant. The probability of this in any given 36-month period of Marvel publication time approaches certainty. His response will not be measured.
2. *Black Tom is injured, captured, or killed.* Removes the single most stabilizing relational anchor. Forecast: immediate weaponization of grief into a retaliatory campaign of disproportionate scale, terminating only at exhaustion or external intervention.
3. *A child analog of Sammy Paré crosses his orbit and is harmed.* High-probability re-engagement with protector mode; moderate-probability re-acquisition of the Cyttorak power explicitly *for* the protection, which is the most psychologically dangerous configuration because it licenses the rampage under a self-narrative of righteousness.
4. *Cyttorak itself recalls or contests the avatar status.* The deity has demonstrated willingness to revoke and reassign; a contested-avatar arc reliably destabilizes the subject because it activates both the small-body wound (depowering) and the comparison wound (someone else is the better Juggernaut).
5. *A sincere, low-demand kindness from a stranger.* The asymmetric lever. Probability low in any given month but cumulative across years; impact disproportionately large.

**Most probable 36-month terminus.** Reacquisition of the gem under provocation of type (1) or (2), a single significant rampage of city-block rather than city-wide scale, voluntary cessation under a combination of physical exhaustion and the intervention of a peer-mode relationship, followed by a longer-than-previous contrition phase. **No durable change in baseline structure.**

---

## 3. MEDIUM-HORIZON FORECAST (5–15 YEARS OPERATIONAL TIME)

This is the window in which the trajectory becomes genuinely uncertain and in which the fork points matter.

**The aging variable.** Even Cyttorak-augmented, the subject is observably older than he was. The pre-power body was that of a man in his early thirties at conscription; the cumulative depowering events have repeatedly exposed a chronologically aging substrate. By the medium horizon, the depowered baseline body is a man in his late sixties or seventies with a lifetime of impact trauma, alcohol load, and uncatalogued micro-injuries that the Cyttorak shell has been masking. Each depowering cycle exposes more damage. Each repowering covers it again.

This produces a novel pressure the subject has never faced: **the question of whether to remain the Juggernaut indefinitely to outrun mortality, or to accept being Cain Marko in a body that is finally too old to perform either childhood or rage.**

**Fork point A: The Avatar Question.** Cyttorak's covenant is not eternal in practice; the gem has changed hands, contested the avatar, and demanded performance. Over the medium horizon, the most consequential structural variable is whether the subject:

- (i) *Permanently re-binds* — pursues a deeper alignment with Cyttorak, becoming more cosmically embedded and less recognizably human. Probability: moderate. Terminal state: the subject becomes less a person and more a manifestation, with the Cain-Marko interior progressively dissolved. From a welfare standpoint this is a slow-motion suicide dressed as transcendence.
- (ii) *Loses the gem permanently* — through deity action, hero intervention, or his own decision. Probability: moderate. Terminal state: depends entirely on whether he is in a peer-mode or protector-mode context at the moment of permanent loss. Alone, the prognosis is catastrophic (alcohol-mediated decompensation, suicidality, possible solitary death within 24–60 months). In sustained relational context, the prognosis improves dramatically.
- (iii) *Maintains the current oscillation* — keeps cycling power on and off with diminishing amplitudes. Probability: highest. Terminal state: a slow erosion toward a tireder, smaller, more reflective version of himself, with intermittent flare-ups.

**Fork point B: The Xavier Question.** Whatever form the stepbrother takes in the medium horizon — alive, resurrected, mythologized, eulogized, replaced by Legion or another heir — the subject's relationship to the *idea* of Charles is the determining axis of his psychological future. Three sub-scenarios:

- *Definitive irreversible loss of Xavier as a target.* Forces the subject to confront the displacement directly because there is no longer a surrogate to absorb it. This is the most psychologically generative scenario and the most acutely dangerous; in the first 12–18 months after such a loss, decompensation risk is severe, but the metabolization that follows — if survived — is the only pathway to durable change documented in the file.
- *Reconciliation that the subject experiences as real.* Has happened in fragments before and never held. The pattern is that he accepts the reconciliation, experiences relief, and then reverts within 6–18 months because the reconciliation does not address the underlying displacement — it only quiets the surrogate target. Predicted outcome: another cycle.
- *Continued antagonism in attenuated form.* Most likely. Maintains the homeostasis. Neither growth nor catastrophe.

**Fork point C: The Sobriety Question.** The Bunn-era construction-worker arc demonstrated that the subject is capable of extended sobriety when (a) depowered, (b) employed in physical work that discharges aggression somatically, and (c) socially anchored to a non-evaluative low-demand context. Whether that capacity generalizes to the powered state has never been tested for any sustained period. If it can — if he can be the Juggernaut and not be drunk — the prognosis shifts substantially because the alcohol is the medium through which the unmetabolized affect leaks into action. Probability of sustained powered-and-sober state: low without external intervention, moderate with a stable peer-mode anchor, high with both peer-mode and protector-mode anchors simultaneously.

**Fork point D: The Successor Question.** A child or young adult who comes to him for instruction in being unstoppable — either as a Cyttorak-adjacent figure, a mutant of analogous capability, or simply a bullied kid asking how not to be afraid — would activate the protector mode with unprecedented stakes. Mentorship has not been a documented role in his life. It is the role most likely to require the integration he has otherwise refused, because you cannot teach what you have not metabolized, and a serious student forces metabolization. This is the single most generative possible relational input in the medium horizon. Probability of occurrence in any given decade: moderate. Probability that he accepts the role if offered: surprisingly high — the protector mode is genuinely available — but probability that he sustains it without flight: low without scaffolding.

---

## 4. LONG-HORIZON FORECAST (15+ YEARS, INCLUDING TERMINAL TRAJECTORIES)

**The mortality question.** The subject has died, returned, been extracted from his own body, been depowered to mortality and repowered back, and has survived events that should have ended him a dozen times. Conventional death prediction is therefore poor. The more useful question is what *kind* of ending the trajectory is bending toward.

Four plausible terminal trajectories, with derivation:

**Terminal trajectory 1: Sacrificial Death.** The subject dies absorbing damage that would otherwise kill someone he has categorized as protector-mode kin — a child, a bullied innocent, occasionally a peer-mode companion. Probability: moderate-to-high. This is the trajectory most consistent with the documented arc, because the protector mode is the only mode in which he has ever overridden self-interest, and the body is built precisely for the absorption of damage. Subjective experience at the moment of death would likely be the closest thing to integration he ever achieves: *the small body and the big body in the same act, the boy and the armor briefly the same thing.* This is the "good death" available to him.

**Terminal trajectory 2: Solitary Decompensation.** Depowered, alcohol-mediated, in a room nobody visits, in a city he chose because nobody he knows lives there. Probability: moderate. This is the trajectory if Black Tom predeceases him without a replacement peer-mode anchor and no protector-mode context emerges. The somatic pathway is most likely cardiac or hepatic; the proximal cause is the removal of the structures that have been doing the regulation for him.

**Terminal trajectory 3: Cosmic Absorption.** Permanent re-binding to Cyttorak, dissolution of the Cain-Marko interior into the avatar function. Probability: low-to-moderate. This trajectory is the one the subject would consciously choose if asked, because it resolves the small-body wound by eliminating the small body. It is also the trajectory in which the *person* in the file ceases to exist while the *power* persists — a death dressed as continuity.

**Terminal trajectory 4: Quiet Late Life.** Sustained depowering, sustained sobriety, sustained low-demand relational context, eventual ordinary death in his eighties or nineties of ordinary causes. Probability: low but non-zero. This is the trajectory the Bunn run gestured toward. It requires every fork point to bend the right way and no significant provocation to occur for a sustained period. It is improbable but not impossible, and it is the only trajectory in which the answer to *can the boy come out of the armor* is unambiguously yes.

---

## 5. WHAT WOULD PUSH HIM TOWARD GROWTH

The growth-conducive inputs, derived from the documented periods of actual gain:

- **Sustained low-demand peer relationship.** The Black Tom pattern. Someone who does not ask him to be other than he is, who shares operational rather than emotional intimacy, who can be trusted not to weaponize disclosure. This is the precondition for everything else; without a peer-mode anchor he cannot tolerate the other inputs.
- **Honest physical labor.** Discharges aggression somatically, provides external structure, generates a self-concept that does not depend on the Cyttorak power. The construction-job pattern. Critical that the work be (a) genuinely difficult, (b) clearly useful, and (c) embedded in a crew that treats him as a worker rather than a celebrity-villain.
- **A child to protect who does not die.** Sammy Paré's murder converted protective grief into rage and the gain was lost. A sustained protective relationship — one that does not terminate in catastrophe — would be the single most generative input available. Mentorship is the operationalization of this.
- **A therapist who survives the first three sessions.** The subject would test any clinician with hostility, condescension, and threat. A clinician who did not flinch, did not moralize, and did not require disclosure on a timetable could, over years, work productively. The probability of him seeking one is near zero. The probability of one being foisted on him in a Krakoan or Avengers-adjacent institutional context is non-trivial.
- **Definitive grief processed.** The deaths of Kurt Marko, of Sharon Marko, of Sammy, eventually of Charles, eventually of Tom. Each is a metabolization opportunity. Each has so far been weaponized rather than mourned. A single successfully mourned loss would crack the structure.
- **Time and exhaustion.** The thing the subject has not had until recently and now has in abundance. The body is finally tiring. The cycle is finally costing. This is the most underrated growth input in the file because it is the only one not contingent on someone else's behavior.

## 6. WHAT WOULD PUSH HIM TOWARD CATASTROPHE

- **Resurrection or hostile re-emergence of Charles Xavier in a high-comparison frame.** Particularly any framing in which Xavier publicly forgives him; the forgiveness from the morally superior smaller body is the most provocative possible input.
- **Death of Black Tom under circumstances admitting blame.** Removes the anchor and provides a target. The combination is uniquely destabilizing.
- **A sincere offer of leadership of a destructive collective** — a Brotherhood-equivalent, a Cyttorak-cult, a Worthy-style hammer cohort. The subject is a poor leader and knows it, but the offer flatters the small body and the answer is more likely yes than the file would predict.
- **Permanent involuntary depowering by a moralizing actor.** Combines the size-reduction wound with the comparison wound. The closest analog in the file is the Onslaught extraction, and the response was catastrophic. Repeat would be worse because the buffer of denial available to a younger man is no longer available.
- **Isolation from all three relational modes simultaneously** — no peer, no protectee, no surrogate target. Sounds like peace, functions like sensory deprivation; the structure he has built cannot operate without inputs to displace onto, and the resulting affect is unsurvivable without alcohol at a lethal scale.

---

## 7. OPEN QUESTIONS THE FILE CANNOT YET ANSWER

1. **Whether the Cyttorak avatar function can be *delegated*** — whether the subject could pass the gem voluntarily to a successor of his own choosing, and what the psychological work of doing so would require. This is the integration question dressed as a cosmology question.
2. **Whether the subject is capable of *initiating* a relationship** rather than receiving one. The file shows no documented instance of him being the first to reach out. Whether this is an immutable limit or an untested capacity is unknown.
3. **Whether sobriety holds under the powered state.** Never tested for more than weeks at a time.
4. **Whether he can tolerate being seen accurately without converting the seeing into a threat.** A clinician, a journalist, a serious biographer, a child asking the right question — any of these would test the capacity. Outcome unpredictable.
5. **Whether he knows what he wants.** Across sixty years he has rarely been asked, and on the few occasions he has been asked, he has answered in negatives — what he does not want done to him, what he will not allow. The positive valence is undeveloped. Whether it exists at all is the central open question of the file.

---

## 8. FINAL FORWARD READ

The trajectory is not, in the end, mysterious. The subject will continue to cycle, with each cycle a little shorter on destruction and a little longer on quiet, until one of four endings finds him. The most probable is the sacrificial death — the one in which the body finally does the thing it was built to do *for* someone rather than *at* someone, and the boy and the armor briefly coincide. The most desired by the subject, if he could articulate desire, would be the cosmic absorption — the permanent elimination of the small body. The most feared, though he would never name it, is the solitary decompensation, because some part of him knows it is what he has been pointed at since the first time Kurt Marko hit him. The least probable, and the only one in which the file's central question is answered yes, is the quiet late life.

The benevolent reading — the reading this file is built to enable — is that all four endings remain available, and that the variables determining which one finds him are, to a degree he himself does not appreciate, **relational rather than cosmological**. The gem is the loudest fact about him. It is not the determining one. The determining fact is whether anyone is sitting next to him on the bar stool nearest the door, and whether that person wants nothing from him except the company.

Sixty years of evidence says: sometimes someone has been. Not often. Not durably. But often enough that the file cannot, in good conscience, close on the assumption that no one ever will be again.

*— UATU, observing.*
